CORRECTION  Cross section data were corrected for                 20370  1   19

              time-dependent background (measured with C sample), 20370  1   21 
              sample admixtures (O in oxides, isotopic impurities,20370  1   22 
              unrecorded pulse height spectrum fraction below     20370  1   23

              intrinsic efficiency of tank (escape probability).  20370  1   25 
            Resonance parameter extraction with area analysis     20370  1   26 
            code TACASI included corrections for                  20370  1   27 
              self-shielding,                                     20370  1   28 
              multiple interactions (Monte Carlo),                20370  1   29 
              instrumental resolution,                            20370  1   30 
              influence of nearby resonances.                     20370  1   31
